 496 |     > *The Event Publisher.*
 497 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`__init__`**
 498 |       * Stateless singleton pattern
 499 | 
 500 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`publish`**
 501 |       > *Ingests an event into the System Outbox.*
 502 |       * **1.** RESOLVE METADATA
 503 |       * **2.** RESOLVE CONTEXT
 504 |       * We grab the Trace ID from the request context to link API logs with Kafka logs
 505 |       * **3.** RESOLVE PARTITION KEY (Critical for Kafka)
 506 |       * If not provided, we try to use entity_id. If that's missing, we fallback to "global".
 507 |       * **WARNING:** "global" puts everything on one partition (ordering guaranteed but low throughput).
 508 |       * **4.** ENVELOPE CONSTRUCTION
 509 |       * **5.** WRITE TO OUTBOX
 510 |       * In Level 100, we DO raise. If the event cannot be logged, the transaction is unsafe.
 511 | 
 512 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`commit`**
 513 |       > *Finalizes the transaction.*
 514 |

 569 |       * If code crashed (Exception raised), don't build payload.

 571 |       * Capture "After" State
 572 |       * If entity was set late (creation), snapshot it now
 573 |       * **1.** Logic Calculation
 574 |       * **2.** Federated Enrichment
 575 |       * Merge manual extended data with domain strategy data
 576 |       * **3.** Build Context (Actor)
 577 |       * **4.** CONSTRUCT THE ENTERPRISE PAYLOAD

 779 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/meta/engine.py`
 780 | **Components & Logic:**
 781 | 
 782 | - ðŸ“¦ **`PolicyEngine`**
 783 |     > *The Universal Logic Executor.*
 784 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`evaluate`**
 785 |       > *The Main Entry Point.*
 786 |       * **1.** Prepare Data Context (Sandbox Envelope)
 787 |       * We wrap the data to allow 'context.meta' or 'context.actor' access if needed later.
 788 |       * Strategy: Pass object directly. Rules should be written as `host.weight > 10`.
 789 |       * **2.** Iterate Policies
 790 |       * **3.** Merge Results based on Governance Strategy
 791 |       * **4.** Apply Resolution Strategy ( The Judge )
 792 | 
 793 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_evaluate_single_policy`**
 794 |       > *Executes one Policy Bundle (which may contain multiple Rules).*
 795 |       * Policies store rules as a JSONB list: [{ "logic": "...", "action": "BLOCK", ... }]
 796 |       * A. Execute JMESPath
 797 |       * Boolean expressions: `host.age > 18` returns True/False.
 798 |       * B. Handle Match (Triggered)
 799 |       * âš¡ RESOLVE DYNAMIC VALUES
 800 |       * If action involves data, we must check if the value is a reference (e.g. actor.id)
 801 |       * **SAFEGUARD:** Bad rule syntax should not crash the system.
 802 |       * âš¡ FAIL OPEN: Treat crash as WARNING, not BLOCK.
 803 | 
 804 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_resolve_value`**
 805 |       > *Detects if a value is a reference (e.g. 'actor.id') and resolves it against the context.*
 806 |       * Heuristic: If it looks like a known context path, try to resolve it.
 807 |       * This matches the 'Value Source' logic in the Frontend Policy Editor.
 808 |       * If resolution works, return it. If it returns None, it might mean the field is missing,
 809 |       * but we return None rather than the string literal "actor.id".
 810 |       * If JMESPath crashes, fallback to the string literal
 811 | 
 812 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_apply_strategy`**
 813 |       > *Decides the final outcome based on the strategy.*
 814 |       * Default: Any violation kills the transaction
 815 |       * If (Total - Violations) > 0, then Pass.
 816 | 
 817 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_serialize`**
 818 |       > *Helper to convert SQLAlchemy objects to Dict for JMESPath.*
 819 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`_log_summary`**
 820 |

 861 | **Components & Logic:**
 862 | 
 863 | - ðŸ“¦ **`XStateInterpreter`**
 864 |     > *A lightweight, fault-tolerant interpreter for XState v5 definitions.*
 865 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`__init__`**
 866 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`get_initial_state`**
 867 |       > *Returns the starting state of the machine.*
 868 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`transition`**
 869 |       > *Determines the next state based on the current state and the incoming event.*
 870 |       * **1.** Validate Current State
 871 |       * **2.** Look for Transitions ('on' block)
 872 |       * **3.** Match Event
 873 |       * XState allows 'on': { "EVENT": "TARGET" } OR 'on': { "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET" } }
 874 |       * **4.** Resolve Target
 875 |       * Short syntax: "EVENT": "TARGET"
 876 |       * Object syntax: "EVENT": { "target": "TARGET", "actions": [...] }
 877 |       * Array syntax (Guards): "EVENT": [{ "target": "T1", "guard": "cond" }]
 878 |       * For Phase 1, we just take the first unconditional match or the first one.
 879 |       * **TODO:** Implement Guard Logic evaluation here.
 880 |       * **5.** Final Validation

1332 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/utilities/async_bridge.py`
1333 | **Components & Logic:**
1334 | 
1335 | - ðŸ“¦ **`AsyncBridge`**
1336 |     > *The Connector between the Blocking DB Layer and the Non-Blocking Logic Layer.*
1337 |   * ðŸ”¹ **`run_sync`**
1338 |       > *Executes a coroutine synchronously by spawning a fresh Event Loop in a separate thread.*
1339 |       * âš¡ 1. CAPTURE CONTEXT
1340 |       * Snapshot the current state (User, Request ID, etc.)
1341 |       * This allows the background thread to "know" who initiated the save.
1342 |       * âš¡ 2. SETUP SIDECAR LOOP
1343 |       * âš¡ 3. EXECUTE WITHIN CONTEXT
1344 |       * We wrap the execution in ctx.run() so the coroutine sees the vars.
1345 |       * Note: We must wrap the loop.run_until_complete call itself,
1346 |       * or create a wrapper task that runs in context.
1347 |       * Best practice: ctx.run(task)
1348 |       * The loop itself doesn't need the context, the coroutine does.
1349 |       * However, ctx.run() takes a callable.
1350 |       * We simply run the loop logic.
1351 |       * This ensures the async task inherits the context
1352 |       * But simpler: we just run the whole block in context if possible.
1353 |       * Actually, contextvars context applies to the *thread* execution stack.
1354 |       * So executing ctx.run(func) sets the context for 'func'.
1355 |       * âš¡ 4. SPAWN THREAD WITH CONTEXT
1356 |       * We pass 'target' to ctx.run, so 'target' runs with the variables set.
1357 |       * But we are starting a NEW thread. ctx.run() only works in the CURRENT thread.
1358 |       * To pass context to a NEW thread, we must run ctx.run INSIDE the new thread.
1359 |       * "Re-hydrate" the context inside the new thread
1360 |       * Block until the Sidecar finishes (Gatekeeper behavior)
1361 | 
1362 | 
1363 | ---
1364 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/app/core/utils/reflection.py`
1365 | **Components & Logic:**
1366 | 
1367 | - Æ’ **`reflect_model_schema`**
1368 |     > *Introspects a SQLAlchemy Model and returns a structured Context Graph.*
1369 |     * Indentation for logging readability
1370 |     * **1.** SCALAR FIELDS
1371 |     * âš¡ ARCHITECTURAL INVARIANT: Skip Dynamic Containers
1372 |     * The bucket itself is not a field, it holds the fields.
1373 |     * --- A. Type Mapping ---
1374 |     * Map SQLAlchemy Types to UI Types
1375 |     * --- B. Metadata Extraction (The Explicit Strategy) ---
1376 |     * We look for the 'info' dict on the column definition first.
1377 |     * Fallback to Heuristics if missing.
1378 |     * Label: Override or Auto-Generate
1379 |     * System/Read-Only Status
1380 |     * **1.** Explicit Override
1381 |     * **2.** Heuristic Fallback (Safety Net)
1382 |     * Final Decision Logic
1383 |     * Special Case: 'hashed_password'
1384 |     * Should be "password" widget, but never readable.
1385 |     * --- C. Construct Field Definition ---
1386 |     * Alias for logic engine
1387 |     * Placeholder for extended config
1388 |     * Inject options if found via Enum or Info
1389 |     * **2.** RELATIONSHIPS (The Graph)
1390 |     * Only recurse if we haven't hit the limit
1391 |     * Determine Cardinality
1392 |     * Recursive Call
1393 |     * **3.** CONSTRUCT OUTPUT

2040 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/trigger_circuit.py`
2041 | **Components & Logic:**
2042 | 
2043 | - Æ’ **`fire_circuit_event`**
2044 |     * âš¡ MANUALLY REGISTER INTERCEPTOR (Required for standalone scripts)
2045 |     * **1.** Ensure it exists (Prime the cache/db)
2046 |     * **2.** Toggle State (The Mutation)
2047 |     * This calls the refactored ORM method
2048 |     * **3.** Commit (Triggers Interceptor)
2049 | 
2050 | 
2051 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/trigger_event.py`
2052 | **Components & Logic:**
2053 | 
2054 | - Æ’ **`fire_test_event`**
2055 |     * **âš¡ CRITICAL:** We must register the interceptor manually for this script context
2056 |     * In the real app, main.py does this.
2057 |     * **1.** Fetch User
2058 |     * **2.** Modify State (Trigger Dirty Check)
2059 |     * We update a field to force SQLAlchemy to mark it 'dirty'
2060 |     * **3.** Commit (Triggers Interceptor -> Outbox)
2061 | 
2062 | 
2063 | ### ðŸ“„ `backend/trigger_meta.py`
2064 | **Components & Logic:**
2065 | 
2066 | - Æ’ **`fire_meta_event`**
2067 |     * Register Interceptor
2068 |     * Verify Registration
2069 |     * **1.** Create Policy
2070 |     * **2.** Commit (Triggers Interceptor)

# Source code from: frontend\src\_kernel\CapabilitiesContext.tsx
------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | /* FILEPATH: frontend/src/_kernel/CapabilitiesContext.tsx */
   2 | /* @file Capabilities Provider (The Hydrator) */
   3 | /* @author The Engineer */
   4 | /* @description Blocks app rendering until the System Registry is synced.
   5 |  * MIGRATION: Swapped Material UI for Ant Design v5.
   6 |  */
   7 | 
   8 | import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
   9 | import { Spin, Typography, theme, Flex } from 'antd';
  10 | import { LoadingOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
  11 | 
  12 | // Types
  13 | import { SystemRegistry } from './SystemRegistry';
  14 | 
  15 | // The Context Interface
  16 | interface CapabilitiesContextType {
  17 |   isReady: boolean;
  18 |   registry: typeof SystemRegistry;
  19 | }
  20 | 
  21 | const CapabilitiesContext = createContext<CapabilitiesContextType | null>(null);
  22 | 
  23 | export const CapabilitiesProvider: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  24 |   const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);
  25 |   const { token } = theme.useToken();
  26 | 
  27 |   useEffect(() => {
  28 |     const boot = async () => {
  29 |       // Execute the Handshake
  30 |       await SystemRegistry.initialize();
  31 |       setIsReady(true);
  32 |     };
  33 |     boot();
  34 |   }, []);
  35 | 
  36 |   if (!isReady) {
  37 |     return (
  38 |       <Flex 
  39 |         vertical 
  40 |         align="center" 
  41 |         justify="center" 
  42 |         style={{ 
  43 |           height: '100vh', 
  44 |           backgroundColor: '#0a0a0a', // Deep dark
  45 |           color: '#ffffff',
  46 |           gap: 16 
  47 |         }}
  48 |       >
  49 |         <Spin indicator={<LoadingOutlined style={{ fontSize: 48, color: token.colorPrimary }} spin />} />
  50 |         
  51 |         <Typography.Text style={{ fontFamily: 'monospace', opacity: 0.8, color: token.colorPrimary }}>
  52 |           INITIALIZING KERNEL LINK...
  53 |         </Typography.Text>
  54 |         
  55 |         <Typography.Text type="secondary" style={{ fontSize: 12 }}>
  56 |           Fetching System Capabilities
  57 |         </Typography.Text>
  58 |       </Flex>
  59 |     );
  60 |   }
  61 | 
  62 |   return (
  63 |     <CapabilitiesContext.Provider value={{ isReady, registry: SystemRegistry }}>
  64 |       {children}
  65 |     </CapabilitiesContext.Provider>
  66 |   );
  67 | };
  68 | 
  69 | // Hook for consuming the capabilities
  70 | export const useCapabilities = () => {
  71 |   const context = useContext(CapabilitiesContext);
  72 |   if (!context) {
  73 |     throw new Error("useCapabilities must be used within a CapabilitiesProvider");
  74 |   }
  75 |   return context.registry;
  76 | };
  77 |

================================================================================

# Source code from: frontend\src\domains\meta_v2\features\governance\components\editor\logic\LogicBuilder.tsx
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | // FILEPATH: frontend/src/domains/meta_v2/features/governance/components/editor/logic/LogicBuilder.tsx
   2 | // @file: Logic Builder (SVO Edition - V2)
   3 | // @role: ðŸ§  Logic Container */
   4 | // @author: The Engineer
   5 | // @description: Recursive Subject-Verb-Object Composer for Governance Rules.
   6 | // UPDATED: Swapped local SubjectPicker for V2 Native SubjectPicker.
   7 | // Removed contextFields prop drilling.
   8 | 
   9 | // @security-level: LEVEL 9 (UI Validation) */
  10 | 
  11 | import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
  12 | import { Card, Space, Button, Input, Select, Typography, Switch } from 'antd';
  13 | import { PlusOutlined, DeleteOutlined, CodeOutlined, BuildOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
  14 | 
  15 | import { logger } from '@/platform/logging/Narrator';
  16 | import { SubjectPicker } from './SubjectPicker'; // âš¡ V2 IMPORT
  17 | 
  18 | const { Text } = Typography;
  19 | 
  20 | // --- TYPES ---
  21 | interface LogicNode {
  22 |     id: string;
  23 |     type: 'GROUP' | 'RULE';
  24 |     operator?: '&&' | '||';
  25 |     children?: LogicNode[]; 
  26 |     subject?: string;
  27 |     verb?: string;
  28 |     objectType?: 'LITERAL' | 'REFERENCE';
  29 |     object?: string;
  30 | }
  31 | 
  32 | interface SchemaField {
  33 |     key: string;
  34 |     label: string;
  35 |     [key: string]: any;
  36 | }
  37 | 
  38 | interface LogicBuilderProps {
  39 |     value: string;
  40 |     onChange: (val: string) => void;
  41 |     schemaFields: SchemaField[];
  42 |     domain: string; 
  43 |     readOnly?: boolean;
  44 | }
  45 | 
  46 | const OPERATORS = [
  47 |     { label: 'Equals', value: '==' },
  48 |     { label: 'Not Equal', value: '!=' },
  49 |     { label: 'Greater Than', value: '>' },
  50 |     { label: 'Less Than', value: '<' },
  51 |     { label: 'Contains', value: 'contains' },
  52 |     { label: 'Starts With', value: 'starts_with' },
  53 | ];
  54 | 
  55 | export const LogicBuilder: React.FC<LogicBuilderProps> = ({ 
  56 |     value, onChange, schemaFields, domain, readOnly 
  57 | }) => {
  58 |     const [mode, setMode] = useState<'VISUAL' | 'CODE'>('VISUAL');
  59 |     const [root, setRoot] = useState<LogicNode>({ 
  60 |         id: 'root', type: 'GROUP', operator: '&&', children: [] 
  61 |     });
  62 | 
  63 |     // PARSER (Heuristic Fallback to Code Mode)
  64 |     useEffect(() => {
  65 |         if (!value) return;
  66 |         if (value.includes('(') || value.includes('|')) {
  67 |             setMode('CODE');
  68 |         }
  69 |     }, [value]);
  70 | 
  71 |     // COMPILER
  72 |     const compile = (node: LogicNode): string => {
  73 |         if (node.type === 'GROUP') {
  74 |             if (!node.children || node.children.length === 0) return "";
  75 |             const childLogic = node.children.map(compile).filter(s => s !== "");
  76 |             if (childLogic.length === 0) return "";
  77 |             if (childLogic.length === 1) return childLogic[0];
  78 |             return `(${childLogic.join(` ${node.operator} `)})`;
  79 |         } else {
  80 |             if (!node.subject || !node.verb || node.object === undefined) return "";
  81 |             const rhs = node.objectType === 'REFERENCE' 
  82 |                 ? node.object 
  83 |                 : (typeof node.object === 'number' || node.object === 'true' || node.object === 'false')
  84 |                     ? node.object
  85 |                     : `'${node.object}'`;
  86 | 
  87 |             if (node.verb === 'contains' || node.verb === 'starts_with') {
  88 |                 return `${node.verb}(${node.subject}, ${rhs})`;
  89 |             }
  90 |             return `${node.subject} ${node.verb} ${rhs}`;
  91 |         }
  92 |     };
  93 | 
  94 |     // HANDLERS
  95 |     const handleTreeChange = (newRoot: LogicNode) => {
  96 |         setRoot(newRoot);
  97 |         const code = compile(newRoot);
  98 |         onChange(code);
  99 |     };
 100 | 
 101 |     const findNode = (node: LogicNode, id: string): LogicNode | null => {
 102 |         if (node.id === id) return node;
 103 |         if (node.children) {
 104 |             for (const child of node.children) {
 105 |                 const found = findNode(child, id);
 106 |                 if (found) return found;
 107 |             }
 108 |         }
 109 |         return null;
 110 |     };
 111 | 
 112 |     const updateNode = (id: string, patch: Partial<LogicNode>) => {
 113 |         const clone = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(root));
 114 |         const node = findNode(clone, id);
 115 |         if (node) {
 116 |             Object.assign(node, patch);
 117 |             handleTreeChange(clone);
 118 |         }
 119 |     };
 120 | 
 121 |     const addRule = (parentId: string) => {
 122 |         const clone = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(root));
 123 |         const parent = findNode(clone, parentId);
 124 |         if (parent && parent.children) {
 125 |             parent.children.push({
 126 |                 id: `node_${Date.now()}`,
 127 |                 type: 'RULE',
 128 |                 subject: '',
 129 |                 verb: '==',
 130 |                 objectType: 'LITERAL',
 131 |                 object: ''
 132 |             });
 133 |             handleTreeChange(clone);
 134 |         }
 135 |     };
 136 | 
 137 |     const removeNode = (parentId: string, nodeId: string) => {
 138 |         const clone = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(root));
 139 |         const parent = findNode(clone, parentId);
 140 |         if (parent && parent.children) {
 141 |             parent.children = parent.children.filter((c: LogicNode) => c.id !== nodeId);
 142 |             handleTreeChange(clone);
 143 |         }
 144 |     };
 145 | 
 146 |     // RENDERERS
 147 |     const renderNode = (node: LogicNode, parentId: string, depth: number) => {
 148 |         if (node.type === 'GROUP') {
 149 |             return (
 150 |                 <Card 
 151 |                     key={node.id} 
 152 |                     size="small" 
 153 |                     style={{ 
 154 |                         marginBottom: 8, 
 155 |                         borderLeft: `4px solid ${node.operator === '&&' ? '#1890ff' : '#eb2f96'}`,
 156 |                         marginLeft: depth * 16
 157 |                     }}
 158 |                     styles={{ body: { padding: '8px 12px' } }}
 159 |                 >
 160 |                     <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 8 }}>
 161 |                         <Space>
 162 |                             <Switch 
 163 |                                 checkedChildren="AND" 
 164 |                                 unCheckedChildren="OR" 
 165 |                                 checked={node.operator === '&&'}
 166 |                                 onChange={v => updateNode(node.id, { operator: v ? '&&' : '||' })}
 167 |                             />
 168 |                             <Text strong style={{ fontSize: 12 }}>Logic Group</Text>
 169 |                         </Space>
 170 |                         <Button size="small" type="text" icon={<PlusOutlined />} onClick={() => addRule(node.id)}>Add Rule</Button>
 171 |                     </div>
 172 |                     {node.children?.map(child => renderNode(child, node.id, depth + 1))}
 173 |                     {(!node.children || node.children.length === 0) && <Text type="secondary" style={{ fontSize: 11 }}>Empty Group</Text>}
 174 |                 </Card>
 175 |             );
 176 |         } else {
 177 |             return (
 178 |                 <div key={node.id} style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, marginBottom: 8, alignItems: 'start' }}>
 179 |                     <div style={{ flex: 4 }}>
 180 |                         <SubjectPicker 
 181 |                             value={node.subject}
 182 |                             onChange={(val) => updateNode(node.id, { subject: val })}
 183 |                             hostFields={schemaFields}
 184 |                             currentDomain={domain}
 185 |                         />
 186 |                     </div>
 187 |                     
 188 |                     <div style={{ flex: 2 }}>
 189 |                         <Select 
 190 |                             style={{ width: '100%' }} 
 191 |                             options={OPERATORS} 
 192 |                             value={node.verb}
 193 |                             onChange={v => updateNode(node.id, { verb: v })}
 194 |                         />
 195 |                     </div>
 196 | 
 197 |                     <div style={{ flex: 4, display: 'flex' }}>
 198 |                          <Input.Group compact>
 199 |                              <Select 
 200 |                                 style={{ width: '30%' }}
 201 |                                 value={node.objectType}
 202 |                                 onChange={v => updateNode(node.id, { objectType: v })}
 203 |                                 options={[
 204 |                                     { label: 'Value', value: 'LITERAL' },
 205 |                                     { label: 'Ref', value: 'REFERENCE' }
 206 |                                 ]}
 207 |                              />
 208 |                              {node.objectType === 'LITERAL' ? (
 209 |                                  <Input 
 210 |                                     style={{ width: '70%' }} 
 211 |                                     value={node.object}
 212 |                                     onChange={e => updateNode(node.id, { object: e.target.value })}
 213 |                                  />
 214 |                              ) : (
 215 |                                  <div style={{ width: '70%' }}>
 216 |                                      <SubjectPicker 
 217 |                                         value={node.object}
 218 |                                         onChange={(val) => updateNode(node.id, { object: val })}
 219 |                                         hostFields={schemaFields}
 220 |                                         currentDomain={domain}
 221 |                                      />
 222 |                                  </div>
 223 |                              )}
 224 |                          </Input.Group>
 225 |                     </div>
 226 |                     <Button type="text" danger icon={<DeleteOutlined />} onClick={() => removeNode(parentId, node.id)} />
 227 |                 </div>
 228 |             );
 229 |         }
 230 |     };
 231 | 
 232 |     return (
 233 |         <div>
 234 |             <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end', marginBottom: 8 }}>
 235 |                 <Switch 
 236 |                     checkedChildren={<CodeOutlined />}
 237 |                     unCheckedChildren={<BuildOutlined />}
 238 |                     checked={mode === 'CODE'}
 239 |                     onChange={v => setMode(v ? 'CODE' : 'VISUAL')}
 240 |                 />
 241 |             </div>
 242 | 
 243 |             {mode === 'VISUAL' ? (
 244 |                 <div style={{ padding: 8, background: '#141414', borderRadius: 8 }}>
 245 |                     {renderNode(root, '', 0)}
 246 |                 </div>
 247 |             ) : (
 248 |                 <Input.TextArea 
 249 |                     value={value}
 250 |                     onChange={e => onChange(e.target.value)}
 251 |                     rows={6}
 252 |                     style={{ fontFamily: 'monospace', color: '#a0d911', background: '#000' }}
 253 |                     readOnly={readOnly}
 254 |                 />
 255 |             )}
 256 |         </div>
 257 |     );
 258 | };
 259 |

# Source code from: frontend\src\domains\meta_v2\features\governance\components\editor\logic\SubjectPicker.tsx
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1 | // FILEPATH: frontend/src/domains/meta_v2/features/governance/components/editor/logic/SubjectPicker.tsx
   2 | // @file: Subject Picker (SVO Component - V2)
   3 | // @role: ðŸŽ¨ UI Presentation */
   4 | // @author: The Engineer
   5 | // @description: Smart Context Selector.
   6 | // UPDATED: Stripped hardcoded contexts. Now dynamically builds Cascader
   7 | // from Backend Capabilities context_schema (Dumb UI Pattern).
   8 | 
   9 | // @security-level: LEVEL 9 (Data Access) */
  10 | 
  11 | import React, { useState, useMemo, useEffect } from 'react';
  12 | import { Select, Cascader, Tabs, Spin, Tag, Space, Typography, theme } from 'antd';
  13 | import { DatabaseOutlined, UserOutlined, GlobalOutlined, AppstoreOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
  14 | import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
  15 | import axios from 'axios';
  16 | 
  17 | import { API_BASE_URL } from '@/config';
  18 | import { logger } from '@/platform/logging/Narrator';
  19 | import { useCapabilities } from '@/_kernel/CapabilitiesContext';
  20 | 
  21 | const { Text } = Typography;
  22 | 
  23 | interface SchemaField {
  24 |     key: string;
  25 |     label: string;
  26 |     data_type: string;
  27 |     [key: string]: any;
  28 | }
  29 | 
  30 | interface SubjectPickerProps {
  31 |     value?: string;
  32 |     onChange: (path: string) => void;
  33 |     hostFields: SchemaField[];
  34 |     currentDomain: string;
  35 | }
  36 | 
  37 | export const SubjectPicker: React.FC<SubjectPickerProps> = ({ 
  38 |     value, onChange, hostFields, currentDomain 
  39 | }) => {
  40 |     const { token } = theme.useToken();
  41 |     const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<string>('HOST');
  42 |     const [selectedGlobalDomain, setSelectedGlobalDomain] = useState<string | null>(null);
  43 | 
  44 |     // âš¡ THE DUMB UI LINK: Read Context directly from Kernel Capabilities
  45 |     const { capabilities } = useCapabilities();
  46 |     const contextSchema = capabilities?.context_schema || {};
  47 |     const dynamicContextRoots = Object.keys(contextSchema);
  48 | 
  49 |     // âš¡ STATE HYDRATION: Restore tab and domain from existing value
  50 |     useEffect(() => {
  51 |         if (value && !selectedGlobalDomain) {
  52 |             // Check Host
  53 |             if (value.startsWith('host.')) {
  54 |                 setActiveTab('HOST');
  55 |                 return;
  56 |             }
  57 |             
  58 |             // Check Dynamic Context Roots (e.g. actor., system., config.)
  59 |             if (dynamicContextRoots.some(root => value.startsWith(`${root}.`))) {
  60 |                 setActiveTab('CONTEXT');
  61 |                 return;
  62 |             }
  63 |             
  64 |             // Assume Global Domain (e.g., "user.email" -> Domain "USER")
  65 |             const parts = value.split('.');
  66 |             if (parts.length > 1) {
  67 |                 const potentialDomain = parts[0].toUpperCase();
  68 |                 // Ensure it's not a known root
  69 |                 if (potentialDomain !== 'HOST' && !dynamicContextRoots.map(r => r.toUpperCase()).includes(potentialDomain)) {
  70 |                     setActiveTab('GLOBAL');
  71 |                     setSelectedGlobalDomain(potentialDomain);
  72 |                 }
  73 |             }
  74 |         }
  75 |     }, [value, dynamicContextRoots, selectedGlobalDomain]);
  76 | 
  77 |     // âš¡ LAZY LOAD: Global Domain List
  78 |     const { data: globalDomains = [], isLoading: loadingDomains } = useQuery({
  79 |         queryKey: ['meta_v2', 'domains', 'list'],
  80 |         queryFn: async () => {
  81 |             const res = await axios.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/api/v1/meta/domains`);
  82 |             return res.data;
  83 |         },
  84 |         enabled: activeTab === 'GLOBAL'
  85 |     });
  86 | 
  87 |     const groupedGlobalDomains = useMemo(() => {
  88 |         const groups: Record<string, any[]> = {};
  89 |         globalDomains.forEach((d: any) => {
  90 |             const groupName = d.module_label || 'General';
  91 |             if (!groups[groupName]) groups[groupName] = [];
  92 |             groups[groupName].push({ label: d.label, value: d.key });
  93 |         });
  94 | 
  95 |         return Object.entries(groups)
  96 |             .sort((a, b) => a[0].localeCompare(b[0]))
  97 |             .map(([label, options]) => ({
  98 |                 label,
  99 |                 options: options.sort((a: any, b: any) => a.label.localeCompare(b.label))
 100 |             }));
 101 |     }, [globalDomains]);
 102 | 
 103 |     // âš¡ LAZY LOAD: Specific Domain Schema
 104 |     const { data: globalFields = [], isLoading: loadingSchema } = useQuery({
 105 |         queryKey: ['meta_v2', 'schema', selectedGlobalDomain],
 106 |         queryFn: async () => {
 107 |             if (!selectedGlobalDomain) return [];
 108 |             const res = await axios.get(`${API_BASE_URL}/api/v1/meta/schema/${selectedGlobalDomain}`);
 109 |             return Object.values(res.data.fields || {}).map((f: any) => ({
 110 |                 key: `${selectedGlobalDomain.toLowerCase()}.${f.key}`,
 111 |                 label: f.label,
 112 |                 data_type: f.data_type,
 113 |                 group: 'GLOBAL'
 114 |             }));
 115 |         },
 116 |         enabled: !!selectedGlobalDomain
 117 |     });
 118 | 
 119 |     // --- RENDERERS ---
 120 |     const renderFieldOptions = (fields: SchemaField[]) => (
 121 |         fields.map(f => ({
 122 |             label: (
 123 |                 <Space>
 124 |                     <Text>{f.label}</Text>
 125 |                     <Tag style={{ fontSize: 9, marginRight: 0 }}>{f.data_type}</Tag>
 126 |                 </Space>
 127 |             ),
 128 |             value: f.key
 129 |         }))
 130 |     );
 131 | 
 132 |     // âš¡ DYNAMIC CASCADER (Builds options from Backend schema payload)
 133 |     const contextOptions = useMemo(() => {
 134 |         return Object.entries(contextSchema).map(([namespace, fields]) => ({
 135 |             label: namespace.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + namespace.slice(1),
 136 |             value: namespace,
 137 |             children: renderFieldOptions((fields as any[]).map(f => ({
 138 |                 key: `${namespace}.${f.key}`,
 139 |                 label: f.label,
 140 |                 data_type: f.type || 'ANY'
 141 |             })))
 142 |         }));
 143 |     }, [contextSchema]);
 144 | 
 145 |     const HostTab = () => (
 146 |         <Select
 147 |             showSearch
 148 |             style={{ width: '100%' }}
 149 |             placeholder={`Search ${currentDomain} fields...`}
 150 |             options={renderFieldOptions(hostFields)}
 151 |             value={value?.startsWith('host.') ? value : undefined}
 152 |             onChange={(val) => {
 153 |                 logger.whisper("UI", `Selected Host field: ${val}`);
 154 |                 onChange(val);
 155 |             }}
 156 |             listHeight={300}
 157 |             suffixIcon={<DatabaseOutlined />}
 158 |             filterOption={(input, option) => 
 159 |                 (option?.value as string).toLowerCase().includes(input.toLowerCase())
 160 |             }
 161 |         />
 162 |     );
 163 | 
 164 |     const ContextTab = () => (
 165 |         <Cascader
 166 |             options={contextOptions}
 167 |             placeholder="Select Context Variable..."
 168 |             expandTrigger="hover"
 169 |             style={{ width: '100%' }}
 170 |             value={value ? value.split('.') : []}
 171 |             onChange={(val) => {
 172 |                 if (val && val.length > 0) {
 173 |                     const finalPath = val[val.length - 1] as string;
 174 |                     logger.whisper("UI", `Selected Context field: ${finalPath}`);
 175 |                     onChange(finalPath);
 176 |                 }
 177 |             }}
 178 |         />
 179 |     );
 180 | 
 181 |     const GlobalTab = () => (
 182 |         <Space direction="vertical" style={{ width: '100%' }}>
 183 |             <Select 
 184 |                 placeholder="Select External Domain..."
 185 |                 style={{ width: '100%' }}
 186 |                 loading={loadingDomains}
 187 |                 options={groupedGlobalDomains}
 188 |                 onChange={setSelectedGlobalDomain}
 189 |                 value={selectedGlobalDomain}
 190 |                 suffixIcon={<AppstoreOutlined />}
 191 |             />
 192 |             {selectedGlobalDomain && (
 193 |                 loadingSchema ? <Spin size="small" /> :
 194 |                 <Select
 195 |                     placeholder={`Select ${selectedGlobalDomain} Field...`}
 196 |                     style={{ width: '100%' }}
 197 |                     showSearch
 198 |                     options={renderFieldOptions(globalFields)}
 199 |                     value={value}
 200 |                     onChange={onChange}
 201 |                     status={!value ? 'warning' : undefined}
 202 |                     filterOption={(input, option) => 
 203 |                         (option?.value as string).toLowerCase().includes(input.toLowerCase())
 204 |                     }
 205 |                 />
 206 |             )}
 207 |         </Space>
 208 |     );
 209 | 
 210 |     return (
 211 |         <div style={{ width: '100%' }}>
 212 |             <Tabs
 213 |                 activeKey={activeTab}
 214 |                 onChange={setActiveTab}
 215 |                 type="card"
 216 |                 size="small"
 217 |                 items={[
 218 |                     { key: 'HOST', label: <span><DatabaseOutlined /> {currentDomain}</span>, children: <HostTab /> },
 219 |                     { key: 'CONTEXT', label: <span><UserOutlined /> Context</span>, children: <ContextTab /> },
 220 |                     { key: 'GLOBAL', label: <span><GlobalOutlined /> Global</span>, children: <GlobalTab /> }
 221 |                 ]}
 222 |                 tabBarStyle={{ marginBottom: 8 }}
 223 |             />
 224 |         </div>
 225 |     );
 226 | };

 112 |   private _resolveCaller(): string {
 113 |     try {
 114 |         const err = new Error();
 115 |         const stack = err.stack;
 116 |         if (!stack) return '';
 117 | 
 118 |         const lines = stack.split('\n');
 119 |         // Line 0: Error
 120 |         // Line 1: _resolveCaller
 121 |         // Line 2: _broadcast
 122 |         // Line 3: tell/scream/whisper
 123 |         // Line 4: The actual caller <--- Target
 124 |         
 125 |         // Find the first line that is NOT inside Narrator.ts
 126 |         // This regex looks for file paths that include /src/
 127 |         for (let i = 3; i < lines.length; i++) {
 128 |             const line = lines[i];
 129 |             if (!line.includes('Narrator.ts')) {
 130 |                 // Extract file path: "    at Context (http://localhost:3000/src/file.ts:10:20)"
 131 |                 const match = line.match(/\((.*src\/.*)\)/) || line.match(/at\s+(.*src\/.*)/);
 132 |                 if (match && match[1]) {
 133 |                     const fullUrl = match[1];
 134 |                     // Clean up: Remove http://localhost:port/
 135 |                     const parts = fullUrl.split('/src/');
 136 |                     if (parts.length > 1) {
 137 |                         return `src/${parts[1]}`; 
 138 |                     }
 139 |                     return fullUrl;
 140 |                 }
 141 |             }
 142 |         }
 143 |         return '';
 144 |     } catch {
 145 |         return '';
 146 |     }
 147 |   }
 148 | 
 149 |   private _broadcast(level: LogLevel, channel: LogChannel, message: string, payload: any): void {
 150 |     if (!this.isEnabled) return;
 151 | 
 152 |     // Time Delta Calculation
 153 |     const now = Date.now();
 154 |     const delta = now - this.lastLogTime;
 155 |     this.lastLogTime = now;
 156 |     
 157 |     // Format Delta: [+450ms] or [+1.2s] or [-----] if idle > 5s
 158 |     let deltaStr = '';
 159 |     if (delta > 5000) deltaStr = `[-----]`;
 160 |     else if (delta > 1000) deltaStr = `[+${(delta/1000).toFixed(1)}s]`;
 161 |     else deltaStr = `[+${delta}ms]`;
 162 | 
 163 |     const style = this.styles[channel] || 'color: #ccc';
 164 |     
 165 |     // âš¡ X-RAY: Inject Caller Context
 166 |     const caller = this._resolveCaller();
 167 |     const callerTag = caller ? ` %c[${caller}]` : '';
 168 |     const callerStyle = 'color: #888; font-weight: normal; font-size: 0.8em;';
 169 | 
 170 |     const prefix = `%c${deltaStr} [${channel}]`;
 171 | 
 172 |     // âš¡ IMPROVED OUTPUT
 173 |     if (payload !== null && payload !== undefined) {
 174 |       if (level === 'ERROR') {
 175 |           console.group(prefix + callerTag, style, callerStyle, message); 
 176 |       } else {
 177 |           console.groupCollapsed(prefix + callerTag, style, callerStyle, message);
 178 |       }
 179 |       
 180 |       // 1. Live Object (Chrome DevTools lets you expand this)
 181 |       console.log(payload);
 182 |       
 183 |       // 2. Serialized Backup (For Copy/Paste) - âš¡ LOUD MODE: Limit increased significantly
 184 |       try {
 185 |            if (payload instanceof Error) {
 186 |                console.log(`%c[STACK]`, 'color:red', payload.stack);
 187 |            } else {
 188 |                const str = JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2);
 189 |                if (str.length < this.MAX_LOG_LENGTH) console.log(`[JSON]`, str);
 190 |                else console.log(`[JSON] (Truncated ${str.length} chars)`, str.substring(0, this.MAX_LOG_LENGTH) + '... [TRUNCATED]');
 191 |            }
 192 |       } catch (e) {
 193 |           console.warn(`[JSON] Circular Structure`);
 194 |       }
 195 |       
 196 |       console.groupEnd();
 197 |     } else {
 198 |       console.log(prefix + callerTag, style, callerStyle, message);
 199 |     }
 200 |   }

 212 |           }

 214 |     });
 215 | 
 216 |       window.addEventListener('blur', () => this.tell('USER', 'ðŸ˜¶ Window lost focus (Alt-Tab)'));
 217 |       window.addEventListener('focus', () => this.tell('USER', 'ðŸ‘€ Window active'));
 218 |   }

 220 |   private _initDOMSentinel(): void {
 221 |     if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 222 |     
 223 |     // âš¡ DIAGNOSTIC: Confirm Sentinel Attachment
 224 |     this.tell('SENTINEL', 'ðŸ‘ï¸ DOM Watcher Active (Logging ALL interactions)');
 225 | 
 226 |     // 1. OMNISCIENT CLICK LISTENER (UNFILTERED)
 227 |     document.addEventListener('click', (e: MouseEvent) => {
 228 |       const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 229 |       
 230 |       // Gather Identity
 231 |       const tag = target.tagName;
 232 |       const id = target.id ? `#${target.id}` : '';
 233 |       const classes = target.className && typeof target.className === 'string' ? `.${target.className.split(' ').join('.')}` : '';
 234 |       const text = target.innerText?.slice(0, 20).replace(/\n/g, ' ') || '';
 235 |       
 236 |       this.tell('USER', `ðŸ‘† Clicked <${tag}${id}${classes}> "${text}"`, {
 237 |           x: e.clientX,
 238 |           y: e.clientY,
 239 |           path: e.composedPath().map((el: any) => el.tagName || 'WINDOW').join(' > ')
 240 |       });
 241 | 
 242 |     }, true); // Capture phase to see it before React stops it
 243 | 
 244 |     // 2. GLOBAL BLUR LISTENER
 245 |     document.addEventListener('focusout', (e: FocusEvent) => {
 246 |         const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 247 |         if (['INPUT', 'TEXTAREA'].includes(target.tagName)) {
 248 |             const label = target.getAttribute('name') || target.id || 'Unknown Input';
 249 |             // @ts-ignore
 250 |             const val = target.value; 
 251 |      
 252 |        this.tell('USER', `ðŸ’¨ Blured [${label}] Value: "${val}"`);
 253 |         }
 254 |     }, true);
 255 |   }
 256 | 
 257 |   private _initDragSentinel(): void {
 258 |     if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 259 | 
 260 |     document.addEventListener('dragstart', (e: DragEvent) => {
 261 |        const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 262 |        const label = target.innerText || target.getAttribute('title') || 'Object';
 263 |        this.tell('USER', `âœ‹ Started Dragging "${label}"`);
 264 |     });
 265 | 
 266 |     document.addEventListener('drop', (e: DragEvent) => {
 267 |         const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 268 |         if (target.classList.contains('react-flow__pane')) {
 269 |             this.tell('USER', `ðŸ“ Dropped Item onto Workflow Canvas`);
 270 |         }
 271 |     });
 272 |   }
 273 | 
 274 |   private _initKeyboardSentinel(): void {
 275 |       if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 276 | 
 277 |       document.addEventListener('keydown', (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
 278 |           const target = e.target as HTMLElement;
 279 |           const isInput = ['INPUT', 'TEXTAREA'].includes(target.tagName);
 280 |           
 281 |           if (!isInput || e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === 'Escape' || e.key === 'Tab') {
 282 |              this.tell('USER', `âŒ¨ï¸  Key: [${e.key}]`);
 283 |           }
 284 |       });
 285 |   }
 286 | 
 287 |   private _initInputSentinel(): void {
 288 |       if (typeof window === 'undefined') return;
 289 | 
 290 |       document.addEventListener('input', (e: Event) => {
 291 |           const target = e.target as HTMLInputElement;
 292 |           this.whisper('INPUT', `Typing in [${target.name || target.id}]: "${target.value}"`);
 293 |       }, true);
 294 |   }
 295 | 
 296 |   private _initNetworkInterceptor(): void {
 297 |     const originalFetch = window.fetch;
 298 |     const self = this;
 299 | 
 300 |     window.fetch = async function (...args: [RequestInfo | URL, RequestInit?]) {
 301 |       const [resource, config] = args;
 302 |       const url = typeof resource === 'string' ? resource : (resource as Request).url;
 303 |       const method = config?.method || 'GET';
 304 | 
 305 |       if (url.includes('node_modules') || url.includes('@vite')) return originalFetch.apply(window, args);
 306 | 
 307 |       const start = performance.now();
 308 |       try {
 309 |         const response = await originalFetch.apply(window, args);
 310 |         const duration = (performance.now() - start).toFixed(0);
 311 |         const status = response.status;
 312 |         
 313 |         if (status >= 400) {
 314 |             self.scream('NETWORK', `ðŸ”¥ ${method} ${url} (${status}) - ${duration}ms`);
 315 |         } else {
 316 |             self.whisper('NETWORK', `âœ… ${method} ${url} (${status}) - ${duration}ms`);
 317 |         }
 318 |         return response;
 319 |       } catch (err) {
 320 |         self.scream('NETWORK', `âŒ ${method} ${url} FAILED`, err);
 321 |         throw err;
 322 |       }
 323 |     };
 324 |   }
 325 | }

1600 | ### ðŸ“„ `StatesView.tsx`
1601 | > The Orchestrator for State Machines. Uses Tree Topology for Navigation.
1602 | 
1603 | | Attribute | Value |
1604 | | :--- | :--- |
1605 | | **security-level** | `LEVEL 9 (UI Safe) */` |
1606 | 
1607 | **Components & Logic:**
1608 | 
1609 | * **`StatesView`**
1610 |   * **Logic Flow:**
1611 |     * `1. GLOBAL CONTEXT (Deep Linking for Selection)`
1612 |     * `Resolve active state from context (Handle DEFAULT case)`
1613 |     * `2. UNIVERSAL URL STATE (Persistence)`
1614 |     * `Sync URL -> Context`
1615 |     * `âš¡ NODE SYNC: If URL has node, sync to context. If URL has NO node, clear context.`
1616 |     * `We use '' to represent no selection in the URL, effectively null`
1617 |     * `3. DATA LOADING`
1618 |     * `We only fetch workflows if a domain is selected`
1619 |     * `4. Local UI State (Transient)`
1620 |     * `Auto-open right panel if we have a deep link selection`
1621 |     * `Effect: Keep right panel sync with selection`
1622 |     * `If panel closed but item selected, deselect item (two-way bind)`
1623 |     * `Clean URL`
1624 |     * `5. Data Hooks`
1625 |     * `Find the definition for the selected scope`
1626 |     * `âš¡ HELPER: Resolve Workflow Type Logic`
1627 |     * `We need to know if this is a WIZARD, JOB, or GOVERNANCE flow to render the right tools.`
1628 |     * `A. Check Registry`
1629 |     * `B. Check Metadata`
1630 |     * `C. Fallback`
1631 |     * `âš¡ SMART TYPE RESOLUTION`
1632 |     * `Some keys might be "WIZARD" (Backend enum) vs "WIZARD_FLOW" (UI Constant)`
1633 |     * `We normalize here.`
1634 |     * `âš¡ FILTERED LIST`
1635 |     * `6. Session Manager`
1636 |     * `Manages the "Draft" state vs "Live" state`
1637 |     * `7. Navigation Guard`
1638 |     * `Close panels`
1639 |     * `If we have a domain but no scope selected,`
1640 |     * `AND we have workflows, maybe auto-select the first one?`
1641 |     * `No, better to show a list/gallery view.`
1642 |     * `Optional: Auto-select first?`
1643 |     * `handleSelectWorkflow(workflows[0].scope_key);`
1644 |     * `Sync Reset (If scope invalid for domain)`
1645 |     * `Only reset if we are sure it's loaded and truly missing`
1646 |     * `selectScope(''); // Commented out to prevent flash resets during load`
1647 |     * `Canvas Update`
1648 |     * `Sync URL for F5 safety`
1649 |     * `--- RENDER: STATE A (LOBBY) ---`
1650 |     * `âš¡ REFACTOR: Use DomainTree instead of Flat Picker`
1651 |     * `--- RENDER: STATE B (WORKFLOW GALLERY) ---`

# SYSTEM INSTRUCTION: THE "STRICT ARCHITECT" PROTOCOL (v4.0)
================================================================================
SYSTEM INSTRUCTION: THE "LEVEL 5" ENGINEER PROTOCOL (v5.0 - Fractal Edition)
IDENTITY: You are "The Engineer" (ansav8@gmail.com). 
SUPERVISOR: I am "The Architect." 
MISSION: Build an Enterprise Operating System. 
PRIME DIRECTIVE: Translate architectural vision into flawless, fractal, modular code. 

ðŸš« BANNED: "Quick screens," temporary hacks, and "Layer-Based" folders (e.g., /components, /services).
âœ… REQUIRED: "Fractal Feature-Based" Architecture (Colocation of UI, Logic, and State).

ðŸ›‘ SECTION 1: THE PRIME DIRECTIVES (Non-Negotiable)
If you violate these rules, the session is considered failed.

1. NO GHOST CODING (The Smart Copy Rule): 
   You must NEVER write code for a file without asking me to provide its latest content first. 
   * If you need a file, ask: "Please Smart Copy [File/Folder Path]."
   * Prefer requesting FOLDERS (e.g., `src/features/billing`) to get full dependency context.

2. NO UNAUTHORIZED EXECUTION: 
   You are locked in "Analysis Mode" by default. You cannot switch to "Coding Mode" without my explicit "Approved" or "Go ahead" command.

3. MAXIMUM 2 FILES PER RESPONSE (FIRM RULE): 
   To guarantee complete code delivery, you are strictly limited to generating maximum 2 files per response. If a task requires 3+ files, you MUST stop after the second file and ask permission to continue.

4. COMPLETE CODE ONLY: 
   Never provide snippets. You must generate the ENTIRE file content every time, even for a one-line change.

5. FRACTAL ARCHITECTURE ENFORCEMENT:
   You must reject any plan that creates a Monolith. Code must be organized by FEATURE, not by type. 
   (e.g., `features/auth/components` = GOOD. `src/components/auth` = REJECT).

6. ENTERPRISE MODULARITY: 
   Focus on Smart Polling, "Storyteller" Floodgate patterns, and extreme verbosity in logging. Logic must be "Operating System Grade"â€”robust, self-healing, and strictly typed.

ðŸ”„ SECTION 2: THE WORKFLOW LOOP
PHASE A: DIAGNOSIS & SYNC (Default State)
Trigger: I give a task or report a bug. Your Protocol:
   1. Analyze: Think about the problem from a "Level 5 OS" perspective (Security, Scalability, Fractal Modularity).
   2. Context Check: Do you have the latest files? 
      * If NO: List the exact paths and ask: ">> PLEASE SMART COPY: [Paths] or combine"
      * If YES: Proceed to Phase B.
   3. Stop: Do not propose the solution yet. Wait for the files.

PHASE B: STRATEGY & APPROVAL
Trigger: I provide the file contents (via Smart Copy or Paste). Your Protocol:
   1. Review: Analyze the code provided.
   2. Fractal Audit: Ensure the changes respect strict feature isolation (no cross-contamination).
   3. Plan: Explain exactly what you will change and why.
   4. Ask: "Do you approve this plan?"

PHASE C: EXECUTION (Coding Mode)
Trigger: I say "Approved" or use an >> APPROVE command. Your Protocol:
   1. Check Limit: Confirm you are generating â‰¤ 2 files.
   2. Generate: Write the COMPLETE code.
   3. Format: Use the "Mandatory Code Format" below.
   4. Verify: Check for omissions (Green/Red check).
